class="ArticleHeader_article-title__futDC"><h1>Technical Terminology Of Computer</h1></div><div class="ArticleHeader_last_updated_parent__ohhpb"><div><span>Last Updated : </span><span>20 Apr, 2023</span></div><div class="ArticleHeader_last_updated_parent--three_dot_dropdown__yslcL"><div styles="[object Object]"><div class="ArticleThreeDot_threedotcontainer__dfGWD"><div class="ArticleThreeDot_share__OyG4_" style="background-position:0px -26px"></div><div class="ArticleThreeDot_comment__gJfFl" style="background-position:0px 0px"></div><div class="ArticleThreeDot_improve___NFbl" style="background-position:-40px -521px"></div><div class="ArticleThreeDot_threedot-wrapper__q4ELY"><ul class="ArticleThreeDot_threedot__ZQ19q"><li></li><li></li><li></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="MainArticleContent_articleMainContentCss__b_1_R <p>All imported and used to terminologies we are going to discuss over here:</p>

<ol><li><strong>Access Point</strong> <strong>:</strong> &nbsp;<br>This is wireless hardware connection in which networking devices are used which also known as base station which create a wireless operation through a line for broadband network the access is at the local area network LAN.&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Aero :&nbsp;</strong><br>This is the name of Window Vista graphical interface which gives a new look to the users' device the full form of Aero is authentic, energetic, reflective and open.&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Application</strong> <strong>:&nbsp;</strong><br>Any program which is made to perform a special task that is known as application for example Microsoft Word, Excel, PowerPoint etc.&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Backup :</strong> &nbsp;<br>Any file which is copy to different source or device.&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Bandwidth :</strong>&nbsp;<br>Tour connection when we transfer data and for that the measurement it is done through a bandwidth this is calculated in bits per second.&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Binary :&nbsp;</strong><br>This is the basic series of system which has 0 and 1.<br>&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Bit</strong> <strong>:&nbsp;</strong><br>This is the short form of binary digit this is the single series of desert which can be 0 or 1 this is a Smallest unit of computer.&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Bitmap :</strong>&nbsp;<br>The file format which is used for Digital pictures format.&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Bluetooth :</strong>&nbsp;<br>Radio Technology through which electronic devices which is used as a facility without connecting any wire so this is a wireless connectivity.&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Browser :</strong>&nbsp;<br>For ceiling data on the web the software program which is used is called browser Microsoft Internet Explorer, Mozilla Firefox, Netscape Navigator are all browsers.&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Buffer :</strong><br>For storing data on for storing data on a temporary basis which is showing various factors like printing disk access etc this helps in increasing the
